<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">discipulus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a pupil, learner</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">discere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to learn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; akin to <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:doceren.html>docere</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to teach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***discus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:discus.html>discus</a> (107603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:discus.html>discus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δίσκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dískos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the eighteenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:discus.html>discus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:discus.html>discussen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:discus.html>discusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***dissen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dissen.html>dissen</a> (43905)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">diss</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dissen.html>dissen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave, to go away</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to diss (to insult someone by being disrespectful)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:distel.html>distel</a> (83968)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:distel.html>distel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thistil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þistilaz</i>.

***distributie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:distributie.html>distributie</a> (15974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">distribution</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">distributio</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">distribuere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to distribute</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:distributie.html>distributie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:distributie.html>distributies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:distributie.html>distributietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A distribution, the act, process or an instance of distributing or being distributed, including the marketing and logistic senses of wide deliveries.</li>
<li>Publicly controlled assignment/delivery of restricted goods, notably under rationing.</li>
<li>An agency in charge of the above.</li>
<li>Physical transmission of motion or energy.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">distribueerder</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">distribueren</span> <i>verb</i></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:distributeur.html>distributeur</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">distributief</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:distributie.html>distributie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> (31)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>this (neuter); <span class="use-with-mention">referring to a thing or a person <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a> by.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>this</b> house</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>this</b> child</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><br />
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_4">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">demonstrative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> this, this here
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>this</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This pronoun can combine with a preposition to form a pronominal adverb. When this occurs, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> changed into its adverbial/locative counterpart <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i>. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p>
